SUMMARY OF GPS VELOCITIES

This file gives the GPS velocities used and the fits for the model in which permanent strain rates are
allowed in 8 of the blocks.
  
* in first column indicates velocity not used in solution
SITE = Site code
SRCE = Velocity source code (see Table 1)
BLCK = Block code (see Table 3) 
POLE = Pole this site constrains
Longit. = Longitude of site
Latit. = Latitude of site
Ve = East velocity from original source
Vn = North velocity from original source
Se = East velocity sigma from original source
Sn = North velocity sigma from original source
Sne = North-East correlation from original source
Enet = East reference frame adjustment 
Nnet = North reference frame adjustment 
Eref = East velocity in NOAM reference frame
Nref = North velocity in NOAM reference frame
Eela = East velocity from elastic strain
Nela = North velocity from elastic strain
Erot = East velocity from block rotation
Nrot = North velocity from block rotation
Estr = East velocity from permanent strain rate
Nstr = North velocity from permanent strain rate
Eres = East residual velocity
Nres = North residual velocity
Vres = Total residual velocity
Vsig = Velocity uncertainty in direction of Vres
R/S = Vres / Vsig
